7389      * declared {@code Throwable} rather than a narrower subtype.  This ensures
7390      * {@code cleanup} will always be invoked with whatever exception that
7391      * {@code target} throws.  Declaring a narrower type may result in a
7392      * {@code ClassCastException} being thrown by the {@code try-finally}
7393      * handle if the type of the exception thrown by {@code target} is not
7394      * assignable to the first parameter type of {@code cleanup}.  Note that
7395      * various exception types of {@code VirtualMachineError},
7396      * {@code LinkageError}, and {@code RuntimeException} can in principle be
7397      * thrown by almost any kind of Java code, and a finally clause that
7398      * catches (say) only {@code IOException} would mask any of the others
7399      * behind a {@code ClassCastException}.
7400      *
7401      * @param target the handle whose execution is to be wrapped in a {@code try} block.
7402      * @param cleanup the handle that is invoked in the finally block.
7403      *
7404      * @return a method handle embodying the {@code try-finally} block composed of the two arguments.
7405      * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
7406      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code cleanup} does not accept
7407      *          the required leading arguments, or if the method handle types do
7408      *          not match in their return types and their
7409      *          corresponding trailing parameters
7410      *
7411      * @see MethodHandles#catchException(MethodHandle, Class, MethodHandle)
7412      * @since 9
7413      */
7414     public static MethodHandle tryFinally(MethodHandle target, MethodHandle cleanup) {
7415         List<Class<?>> targetParamTypes = target.type().parameterList();
7416         Class<?> rtype = target.type().returnType();
7417 
7418         tryFinallyChecks(target, cleanup);
7419 
7420         // Match parameter lists: if the cleanup has a shorter parameter list than the target, add ignored arguments.
7421         // The cleanup parameter list (minus the leading Throwable and result parameters) must be a sublist of the
7422         // target parameter list.
7423         cleanup = dropArgumentsToMatch(cleanup, (rtype == void.class ? 1 : 2), targetParamTypes, 0);
7424 
7425         // Ensure that the intrinsic type checks the instance thrown by the
7426         // target against the first parameter of cleanup
7427         cleanup = cleanup.asType(cleanup.type().changeParameterType(0, Throwable.class));
7428 
7429         // Use asFixedArity() to avoid unnecessary boxing of last argument for VarargsCollector case.
7430         return MethodHandleImpl.makeTryFinally(target.asFixedArity(), cleanup.asFixedArity(), rtype, targetParamTypes);
7431     }
7432 
7433     private static void tryFinallyChecks(MethodHandle target, MethodHandle cleanup) {
7434         Class<?> rtype = target.type().returnType();
7435         if (rtype != cleanup.type().returnType()) {
7436             throw misMatchedTypes("target and return types", cleanup.type().returnType(), rtype);
7437         }
7438         MethodType cleanupType = cleanup.type();
7439         if (!Throwable.class.isAssignableFrom(cleanupType.parameterType(0))) {
7440             throw misMatchedTypes("cleanup first argument and Throwable", cleanup.type(), Throwable.class);
7441         }
7442         if (rtype != void.class && cleanupType.parameterType(1) != rtype) {
7443             throw misMatchedTypes("cleanup second argument and target return type", cleanup.type(), rtype);
7444         }
7445         // The cleanup parameter list (minus the leading Throwable and result parameters) must be a sublist of the
7446         // target parameter list.
7447         int cleanupArgIndex = rtype == void.class ? 1 : 2;
7448         if (!cleanupType.effectivelyIdenticalParameters(cleanupArgIndex, target.type().parameterList())) {
7449             throw misMatchedTypes("cleanup parameters after (Throwable,result) and target parameter list prefix",
7450                     cleanup.type(), target.type());
7451         }
7452     }
7453
